We want to formilise in HoTT the intuition behind a correspondance between the
concept of PathOver and total spaces. PathOver was briefly mentioned in
{% cite hottbook %} and later defined in {% cite Licata2015 %}.

![](/assets/png-images/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers-7f9fb342.png)

Since pathovers are common in HoTT (See for instance its extensive use in {%
cite hott-in:agda %}), the following stregthen our intution about these types.
Let's review the equility types (See {% cite Licata2015 %}).

## Homogeneous equality

> `Path {A} a₀ a₁` is sometimes called **homogeneous equality**, because it
> relates two elements a₀ and a₁ whose types are *definitionally/judgementally
> equal*.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="977" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="983" class="Number">30</a> <a id="986" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#996" class="Datatype Operator">_==_</a>

## Heterogeneous equality

> In {%cite McBride2004 %} the author introduced a *heterogeneous equality*, which is an equality type
> `a:A= b:B` that relates two elements `a:A` and `b:B` which may have two judgementally
> distinct types, though the reflexivity constructor applies only when both the
> two types and the two terms are judgementally equal.

> However, McBride’s heterogeneous equality is **logically equivalent** to a
> homogeneous equality type *satisfying uniqueness of identity proofs*, which
> is undesirable **in homotopy type theory, because not all types should be sets**.

> This heterogeneous equality relates two elements of two different types along a
> specific equality α between the types

  <a id="9218" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="9225" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9225" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="9234" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9235" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9235" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="9238" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9238" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9240" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9242" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9243" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9243" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9245" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9247" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9252" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9235" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="9254" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9256" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9257" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9257" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9259" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9261" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9243" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9263" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9265" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9270" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9238" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9272" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9274" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="9284" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
    <a id="9364" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
    <a id="hott.Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="9406" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9406" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="9415" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9418" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9418" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9420" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9420" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9422" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9424" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="9426" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9426" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9428" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9430" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9243" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9431" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9433" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9257" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9426" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9438" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9441" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9443" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9448" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9449" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9235" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="9452" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9454" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9238" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9456" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="12984" class="Comment">-- Application of an homotopy</a>

    <a id="13087" class="Comment">-- The axiom of function extensionality postulates that the</a>
    <a id="13151" class="Comment">-- application of homotopies is an equivalence.</a>

  <a id="15894" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="15901" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#15901" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="15914" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="15925" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
    <a id="15996" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
    <a id="hott.Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="16013" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16013" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="16020" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16022" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="16024" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16024" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="16025" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="16028" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16029" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16029" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16031" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16033" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="16038" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16024" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="16039" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16041" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16043" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="16048" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16024" class="Bound">ℓ</a>

    <a id="23256" class="Comment">-- Half-adjointness implies equivalence.</a>
    <a id="hott.Halfadjoints.ishae-≃"></a><a id="23301" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#23301" class="Function">ishae-≃</a> <a id="23309" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23311" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23312" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#23312" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23314" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23316" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20623" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23318" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23320" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20637" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23321" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23323" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23325" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20701" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="23331" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#23312" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23333" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23335" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20623" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23337" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11896" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="23339" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20637" class="Bound">B</a>

    <a id="26054" class="Comment">-- Quasiinverses create equivalences.</a>

### Equivalent Types

Let be `α : A == B`, `a : A`, and `b : B` then the following types are equivalent
to `HEq`.

To complete with the chain of equivalence, we show  `HEq₄-≃-HEq₁`

We will prefer the first definition.

## Path over a path

The following five definition for pathovers are equivalent.

- <pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="32045" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="PathOver₁"></a><a id="32050" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32050" class="Datatype">PathOver₁</a> <a id="32060" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32061" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32061" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="32062" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32064" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32065" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32065" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32067" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32069" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="32073" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32061" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="32074" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32076" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32077" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32077" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="32079" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32081" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32065" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32083" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32085" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="32090" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32061" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="32091" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32093" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32094" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32094" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="32097" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32099" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32065" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32100" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32102" class="Symbol">:</a>

class="Bound">A</a><a id="32919" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32921" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32922" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32922" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="32924" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32926" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32910" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="32929" href="{% endraw %}{% link id="32934" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32936" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32937" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32937" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="32940" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32942" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32890" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="32944" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32910" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="32946" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32948" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32949" href="{% endraw %}{% link <a id="32962" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="32967" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32871" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a>
<a id="32970" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32853" class="Function">PathOver₅</a> <a id="32980" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32981" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="32983" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="32985" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32985" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32986" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32988" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32988" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="32990" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1047" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="32994" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32994" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="32997" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32997" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="33000" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33002" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32994" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="33005" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#996" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="33008" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32997" class="Bound">c₂</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Above when we used `transport C α c₁`, we could also have used `coe (ap C α)`,
both functions are of type `C a₁ → C a₂`. The other case with `c₂` is similar.


{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="33210" class="Comment">-- PathOver₃ is equivalent to PathOver₅</a>
<a id="33250" class="Comment">-- The proof is using quasiinverse,</a>

    <a id="33887" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="33899" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33899" class="Function">₃~₅</a> <a id="33903" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33905" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33906" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33906" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="33908" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33910" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32853" class="Function">PathOver₅</a> <a id="33920" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33313" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="33922" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1047" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="33926" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33838" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="33929" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33842" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="33931" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="33943" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33341" class="Function">₃-to-₅</a> <a id="33952" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33953" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33518" class="Function">₅-to-₃</a> <a id="33960" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33906" class="Bound">p</a><a id="33961" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33963" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#996" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="33966" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33906" class="Bound">p</a>

      <a id="33995" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33995" class="Function">₅~₃</a> <a id="33999" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34001" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34002" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34002" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="34004" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34006" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32454" class="Function">PathOver₃</a> <a id="34016" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33313" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="34018" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33824" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="34021" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33824" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="34024" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1047" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="34028" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33838" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="34031" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33842" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="34033" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="34076" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33995" class="Function">₅~₃</a> <a id="34080" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1047" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="34084" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34086" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1047" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


We are going to use the fifth definition for pathovers, the one which is
using an inductive family.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="34216" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34216" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="34225" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34227" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#32853" class="Function">PathOver₅</a>

<a id="34238" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="34244" class="Number">30</a> <a id="34247" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34216" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="34256" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="34263" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34216" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="34280" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>


> While we have motivated PathOver as a factored heterogeneous equality, there
> is also a geometric intuition. **Dependent types correspond to fibrations**, so a
> type `C : A → Type` can be pictured as its total space `∑ a:A . C` a projecting
> down to `A` by first projection.

> A **path-over** `γ : PathOver C α c­₁ c₂` represents a path σ in `∑ a:A . C` a
> a between `(a₁, c₁)` and `(a₂,c₂)`, such that ap fst σ is exactly `α`. That
> is, it is a path in the total space that projects down to, or lies over, `α`
> (path pairing `pair= α γ` will be made precise below)


## Total spaces

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="34919" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="34926" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34926" class="Module">_</a> <a id="34928" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34929" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34929" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="34931" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34931" class="Bound">j</a><a id="34932" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="34934" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34934" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34936" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34938" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="34943" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34929" class="Bound">i</a><a id="34944" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="34946" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34946" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34948" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34950" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34934" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34952" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34954" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="34959" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34931" class="Bound">j</a><a id="34960" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="34962" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34962" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34964" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34964" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="34966" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34968" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-Pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34934" class="Bound">A</a><a id="34969" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="34971" class="Keyword">where</a>
